"text": "<user_message>\nDesign a comprehensive architecture for a self-hosted Roo Code Cloud API, to be placed in the `self-hosted-cloudapi/` directory at the root of the Roo-Code repository.\n\n## Context\n\nThe Roo Code VS Code extension communicates with a cloud API for authentication, settings, telemetry, task sharing, marketplace, and LLM proxying. We need to build a self-hosted replacement that is compatible with the existing Roo Code client.\n\n## Technology Stack Requirements\n- **Language**: Python\n- **Framework**: FastAPI\n- **Database**: PostgreSQL (with SQLAlchemy ORM + Alembic migrations)\n- **Auth**: Authentik for OAuth (replacing Clerk)\n- **Deployment**: Docker + docker-compose\n\n## Key Findings from Codebase Analysis\n\nThe Roo Code client communicates with three API surfaces:\n\n### 1. Roo Code API (`app.roocode.com`) — Main Cloud API\nAll endpoints use `Authorization: Bearer {sessionToken}` header:\n\n| Endpoint | Method | Description |\n|---|---|---|\n| `/api/extension/share` | POST | Share a task — body: `{ taskId, visibility }`, returns `ShareResponse` |\n| `/api/extension/bridge/config` | GET | Get bridge/websocket config — returns `{ userId, socketBridgeUrl, token }` |\n| `/api/extension/credit-balance` | GET | Get credit balance — returns `{ balance: number }` |\n| `/api/extension-settings` | GET | Fetch org + user settings — returns `{ organization: OrganizationSettings, user: UserSettingsData }` |\n| `/api/user-settings` | PATCH | Update user settings — body: `{ settings, version }`, returns `UserSettingsData` |\n| `/api/events` | POST | Record telemetry event |\n| `/api/events/backfill` | POST | Backfill task messages (FormData) |\n| `/api/marketplace/modes` | GET | Fetch mode marketplace (unauthenticated) |\n| `/api/marketplace/mcps` | GET | Fetch MCP marketplace (unauthenticated) |\n\n### 2. Clerk Auth API (`clerk.roocode.com`) — Authentication\nThe client currently uses Clerk for auth. We need a **Clerk-compatible facade** so the client works without modification:\n\n| Endpoint | Method | Description |\n|---|---|---|\n| `/v1/client/sign_ins` | POST | Sign in (ticket strategy) |\n| `/v1/client/sessions/{id}/tokens` | POST | Create session JWT |\n| `/v1/me` | GET | Get user profile |\n| `/v1/me/organization_memberships` | GET | Get org memberships |\n| `/v1/client/sessions/{id}/remove` | POST | Logout/remove session |\n\n**Browser login URLs** (the client opens these in a browser):\n- `{apiUrl}/extension/sign-in?state={csrf}&auth_redirect={vscode://...}`\n- `{apiUrl}/extension/provider-sign-up?state={csrf}&auth_redirect={vscode://...}`\n- `{apiUrl}/l/{landingPageSlug}?state={csrf}&auth_redirect={vscode://...}`\n\n**JWT Payload Structure** (the client validates this):\n`typescript\ninterface JWTPayload {\n  iss?: string       // Issuer (should be 'rcc')\n  sub?: string       // Subject - User ID for auth tokens (t:'auth')\n  exp?: number       // Expiration time\n  iat?: number       // Issued at time\n  v?: number         // Version (should be 1)\n  r?: {\n    u?: string       // User ID\n    o?: string       // Organization ID (optional)\n    t?: string       // Token type: 'auth' for auth tokens\n  }\n}\n`\n\n**Auth flow**: Client opens browser → browser redirects to Authentik OAuth → Authentik callback → our server issues Clerk-compatible JWT → client receives code via URI callback → client calls `/v1/client/sign_ins` with ticket → gets session → refreshes via `/v1/client/sessions/{id}/tokens` every ~50 seconds.\n\n### 3. Provider Proxy API (`api.roocode.com/proxy`) — LLM Proxy\nOpenAI-compatible proxy:\n\n| Endpoint | Method | Auth | Description |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `/v1/chat/completions` | POST (streaming) | Bearer sessionToken | OpenAI-compatible chat completions |\n| `/v1/models` | GET | Bearer (optional) | List available models (RooModelsResponse schema) |\n| `/v1/images/generations` | POST | Bearer sessionToken | Image generation |\n\n**RooModelsResponse schema**:\n`typescript\n{\n  object: \"list\",\n  data: [{\n    id: string,\n    object: \"model\",\n    created: number,\n    owned_by: string,\n    name: string,\n    description: string,\n    context_window: number,\n    max_tokens: number,\n    type: \"language\",\n    tags?: string[],  // \"vision\", \"reasoning\", \"reasoning-required\", \"stealth\", \"free\"\n    pricing: { input: number, output: number, input_cache_read?: number, input_cache_write?: number },\n    deprecated?: boolean,\n    default_temperature?: number,\n    settings?: Record<string, unknown>,\n    versionedSettings?: Record<string, Record<string, unknown>>\n  }]\n}\n`\n\n### Environment Variables the Client Uses\n- `ROO_CODE_API_URL` → point to self-hosted API\n- `CLERK_BASE_URL` → point to auth server (our Clerk-compatible facade)\n- `ROO_CODE_PROVIDER_URL` → point to LLM proxy\n- `ROO_CODE_CLOUD_TOKEN` → for static token auth (agents)\n- `ROO_CODE_CLOUD_ORG_SETTINGS` → base64-encoded JSON org settings (static override)\n- `ROO_CODE_DISABLE_TELEMETRY=1` → disable telemetry\n\n### Data Models (Key Types)\n\n**CloudUserInfo**: `{ id, name, email, picture, organizationId, organizationName, organizationRole, organizationImageUrl }`\n\n**OrganizationSettings**: `{ version, cloudSettings: { recordTaskMessages, enableTaskSharing, allowPublicTaskSharing, taskShareExpirationDays, allowMembersViewAllTasks, workspaceTaskVisibility, llmEnhancedFeaturesEnabled }, defaultSettings, allowList, features, hiddenMcps, hideMarketplaceMcps, mcps, providerProfiles }`\n\n**UserSettingsData**: `{ features: UserFeatures, settings: { taskSyncEnabled, llmEnhancedFeaturesEnabled }, version }`\n\n**ShareResponse**: `{ success, shareUrl, error, isNewShare, manageUrl }`\n\n**UsageStats**: `{ success, data: { dates, tasks, tokens, costs, totals }, period }`\n\n## Architecture Design Requirements\n\nPlease design the architecture covering:\n\n1. **Project Structure**: Directory layout for the Python project\n2. **Auth System**: How to implement a Clerk-compatible auth facade backed by Authentik OAuth\n - Authentik OAuth flow (authorization code + PKCE)\n - Clerk-compatible JWT issuance with the exact payload structure the client expects\n - Session management (create, refresh, destroy)\n - Static token support (for `ROO_CODE_CLOUD_TOKEN`)\n - Browser sign-in/sign-up flow that redirects through Authentik\n3. **Database Schema**: PostgreSQL tables for users, organizations, memberships, settings, tasks, shares, events, etc.\n4. **API Layer**: FastAPI routers for each endpoint group\n5. **LLM Proxy**: How the proxy forwards requests to upstream LLM providers (OpenAI, Anthropic, etc.) and returns OpenAI-compatible responses\n6. **Configuration**: Environment variables, settings management\n7. **Docker**: docker-compose with API, PostgreSQL, and integration points for Authentik\n8. **Security**: CORS, rate limiting, input validation\n9. **Marketplace**: How mode/MCP marketplace data is served (YAML/JSON files or database)\n\nCreate the architecture document at `plans/self-hosted-cloud-api-architecture.md`.\n\nThis task should ONLY produce the architecture plan document. Do not implement any code. Use `attempt_completion` when done to provide a summary of the architecture.\n</user_message>"

Let me summarize what I've learned:\n\n1. **Auth System (Clerk-compatible)**:\n   - Client uses`WebAuthService`which calls Clerk API endpoints:\n     -`POST /v1/client/sign_ins`with`strategy=ticket`and`ticket=<code>`→ returns`created_session_id`and`Authorization`header with client token\n     -`POST /v1/client/sessions/{id}/tokens`with`\_is_native=1`and optional`organization_id`→ returns JWT\n     -`GET /v1/me`→ returns user profile (id, first_name, last_name, image_url, email_addresses)\n     -`GET /v1/me/organization_memberships`→ returns org memberships\n     -`POST /v1/client/sessions/{id}/remove`→ logout\n   - JWT payload structure:`{ iss, sub, exp, iat, nbf, v, r: { u, o, t } }`where`t`is 'auth' or 'cj'\n   - Auth flow: Browser opens sign-in URL → OAuth → callback with`code`and`state`→ client calls`/v1/client/sign_ins`with ticket → gets session → refreshes every ~50s\n   - URI callback:`/auth/clerk/callback?code=...&state=...&organizationId=...&provider_model=...`\n   - Static token auth via `ROO_CODE_CLOUD_TOKEN`env var (StaticTokenAuthService)\n\n2. **Cloud API Endpoints**:\n   -`POST /api/extension/share`- Share task\n   -`GET /api/extension/bridge/config`- Bridge/websocket config\n   -`GET /api/extension/credit-balance`- Credit balance\n   -`GET /api/extension-settings`- Org + user settings\n   -`PATCH /api/user-settings`- Update user settings\n   -`POST /api/events`- Record telemetry event\n   -`POST /api/events/backfill`- Backfill task messages (FormData)\n   -`GET /api/marketplace/modes`- Mode marketplace (unauthenticated)\n   -`GET /api/marketplace/mcps`- MCP marketplace (unauthenticated)\n\n3. **LLM Proxy**:\n   - Base URL:`ROO_CODE_PROVIDER_URL`or`https://api.roocode.com/proxy`\n - Client appends `/v1` to base URL\n - Endpoints: `/v1/chat/completions` (streaming), `/v1/models`, `/v1/images/generations`\n - Uses `Authorization: Bearer {sessionToken}` header\n - Models response follows `RooModelsResponseSchema`\n\n4. **Environment Variables**:\n - `ROO_CODE_API_URL` → main API URL\n - `CLERK_BASE_URL` → auth server URL\n - `ROO_CODE_PROVIDER_URL` → LLM proxy URL\n - I need to cover:\n\n1. **Project Structure** - Directory layout for the Python project\n2. **Auth System** - Clerk-compatible auth facade backed by Authentik OAuth\n3. **Database Schema** - PostgreSQL tables\n4. **API Layer** - FastAPI routers\n5. **LLM Proxy** - How the proxy forwards requests\n6. **Configuration** - Environment variables\n7. **Docker** - docker-compose\n8. **Security** - CORS, rate limiting, input validation\n9. **Marketplace** - How marketplace data is served\n\nLet me synthesize everything I've learned from the codebase analysis:\n\n### Key findings:\n\n**Auth Flow (from WebAuthService.ts):**\n1. Client opens browser to `{apiUrl}/extension/sign-in?state={csrf}&auth_redirect={vscode://...}`\n2. Browser authenticates via Authentik OAuth\n3. Authentik callback redirects to our server\n4. Our server issues a \"ticket\" code\n5. Browser redirects to VS Code URI: `vscode://...?code={ticket}&state={csrf}`\n6. Client calls `POST /v1/client/sign_ins` with `strategy=ticket&ticket={code}` → gets `clientToken` (from Authorization header) and `sessionId` (from response body `created_session_id`)\n7. Client calls `POST /v1/client/sessions/{sessionId}/tokens` with `_is_native=1` and optional `organization_id` → gets JWT\n8. Client refreshes JWT every ~50 seconds\n9. Client calls `GET /v1/me` with clientToken → gets user profile\n10. Client calls `GET /v1/me/organization_memberships` → gets org memberships\n11. Client calls `POST /v1/client/sessions/{sessionId}/remove` → logout\n\n**JWT Payload Structure (from types/cloud.ts):**\n`typescript\ninterface JWTPayload {\n  iss?: string       // Issuer (should be 'rcc')\n  sub?: string       // Subject - User ID for auth tokens (t:'auth')\n  exp?: number       // Expiration time\n  iat?: number       // Issued at time\n  nbf?: number       // Not before time\n  v?: number         // Version (should be 1)\n  r?: {\n    u?: string       // User ID (always present in valid tokens)\n    o?: string       // Organization ID (optional - undefined when orgId is null)\n    t?: string       // Token type: 'cj' for job tokens, 'auth' for auth tokens\n  }\n}\n`\n\n**StaticTokenAuthService (from StaticTokenAuthService.ts):**\n- Decodes JWT to extract `r.u` (user ID), `r.o` (org ID), `sub` (fallback user ID)\n- Uses `ROO_CODE_CLOUD_TOKEN` env var\n- Always returns \"active-session\" state\n\n**API Endpoints (from CloudAPI.ts, CloudSettingsService.ts, TelemetryClient.ts, RemoteConfigLoader.ts):**\n- `POST /api/extension/share` - Share task\n- `GET /api/extension/bridge/config` - Bridge/websocket config\n- `GET /api/extension/credit-balance` - Credit balance\n- `GET /api/extension-settings` - Org + user settings\n- `PATCH /api/user-settings` - Update user settings\n- `POST /api/events` - Record telemetry event\n- `POST /api/events/backfill` - Backfill task messages (FormData)\n- `GET /api/marketplace/modes` - Mode marketplace (unauthenticated)\n- `GET /api/marketplace/mcps` - MCP marketplace (unauthenticated)\n\n**Clerk API Endpoints (from WebAuthService.ts):**\n- `POST /v1/client/sign_ins` - Sign in (ticket strategy, form-urlencoded)\n - Body: `strategy=ticket&ticket={code}`\n - Response: `{ response: { created_session_id: string } }`\n - Header: `Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}` (extracted from response)\n- `POST /v1/client/sessions/{id}/tokens` - Create session JWT (form-urlencoded)\n - Body: `_is_native=1&organization_id={orgId or empty}`\n - Header: `Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}`\n - Response: `{ jwt: string }`\n- `GET /v1/me` - Get user profile\n - Header: `Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}`\n - Response: `{ response: { id, first_name, last_name, image_url, primary_email_address_id, email_addresses: [{id, email_address}], public_metadata } }`\n- `GET /v1/me/organization_memberships` - Get org memberships\n - Header: `Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}`\n - Response: `{ response: [{ id, role, permissions, organization: { id, name, slug, image_url, has_image, created_at, updated_at } }] }`\n- `POST /v1/client/sessions/{id}/remove` - Logout (form-urlencoded)\n - Body: `_is_native=1`\n - Header: `Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}`\n\n**Provider Proxy (from roo.ts):**\n- `POST /v1/chat/completions` - Streaming chat completions (OpenAI-compatible)\n- `GET /v1/models` - List models (RooModelsResponse schema)\n- `POST /v1/images/generations` - Image generation\n\n**RooModelsResponse schema (from providers/roo.ts):**\n`typescript\n{\n  object: \"list\",\n  data: [{\n    id: string,\n    object: \"model\",\n    created: number,\n    owned_by: string,\n    name: string,\n    description: string,\n    context_window: number,\n    max_tokens: number,\n    type: \"language\",\n    tags?: string[],  // \"vision\", \"reasoning\", \"reasoning-required\", \"stealth\", \"free\"\n    pricing: { input: string, output: string, input_cache_read?: string, input_cache_write?: string },\n    deprecated?: boolean,\n    default_temperature?: number,\n    settings?: Record<string, unknown>,\n    versionedSettings?: Record<string, Record<string, unknown>>\n  }]\n}\n`\n\n**URI Handler (from handleUri.ts):**\n- `/auth/clerk/callback` - Auth callback with `code`, `state`, `organizationId`, `provider_model` params\n\n**Environment Variables:**\n- `ROO_CODE_API_URL` → point to self-hosted API\n- `CLERK_BASE_URL` → point to auth server (our Clerk-compatible facade)\n- `ROO_CODE_PROVIDER_URL` → point to LLM proxy\n- `ROO_CODE_CLOUD_TOKEN` → for static token auth (agents)\n- `ROO_CODE_CLOUD_ORG_SETTINGS` → base64-encoded JSON org settings\n- `ROO_CODE_DISABLE_TELEMETRY=1` → disable telemetry\n\nNow let me write the comprehensive architecture document.",

"content": "# Self-Hosted Roo Code Cloud API — Architecture Plan\n\n## 1. Overview\n\nThis document describes the architecture for a self-hosted replacement of the Roo Code Cloud API, placed in the `self-hosted-cloudapi/` directory at the root of the Roo-Code repository. The server is a Python/FastAPI application that provides a **Clerk-compatible authentication facade** backed by Authentik OAuth, the **main Roo Code API** endpoints, and an **LLM proxy** — all compatible with the existing Roo Code VS Code extension client without modification.\n\nThe client connects to three API surfaces, controlled by three environment variables:\n\n| Env Variable | Default Production URL | Self-Hosted Target |\n|---|---|---|\n| `CLERK_BASE_URL` | `https://clerk.roocode.com` | Our Clerk-compatible auth facade |\n| `ROO_CODE_API_URL` | `https://app.roocode.com` | Our main API |\n| `ROO_CODE_PROVIDER_URL` | `https://api.roocode.com/proxy` | Our LLM proxy |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Project Structure\n\n`\nself-hosted-cloudapi/\n├── README.md\n├── pyproject.toml                    # Poetry/pip project definition\n├── alembic.ini                       # Alembic migration config\n├── Dockerfile\n├── docker-compose.yml\n├── .env.example\n│\n├── alembic/\n│   ├── env.py\n│   ├── script.py.mako\n│   └── versions/\n│       └── 001_initial_schema.py\n│\n├── config/\n│   ├── __init__.py\n│   ├── settings.py                  # Pydantic Settings (env vars)\n│   ├── auth.py                      # Auth-related config helpers\n│   └── marketplace/                 # Static marketplace data\n│       ├── modes.yaml\n│       └── mcps.yaml\n│\n├── src/\n│   ├── __init__.py\n│   ├── main.py                      # FastAPI app factory, lifespan, middleware\n│   ├── dependencies.py              # FastAPI dependency injection\n│   │\n│   ├── models/                      # SQLAlchemy ORM models\n│   │   ├── __init__.py\n│   │   ├── base.py                  # DeclarativeBase, common mixins\n│   │   ├── user.py                  # User, Session, ClientToken\n│   │   ├── organization.py          # Organization, Membership\n│   │   ├── settings.py              # OrganizationSettings, UserSettings\n│   │   ├── task.py                  # Task, TaskShare, TaskMessage\n│   │   ├── event.py                 # TelemetryEvent\n│   │   └── marketplace.py           # MarketplaceEntry (if DB-driven)\n│   │\n│   ├── schemas/                     # Pydantic request/response schemas\n│   │   ├── __init__.py\n│   │   ├── auth.py                  # Clerk-compatible response schemas\n│   │   ├── settings.py              # Org/user settings schemas\n│   │   ├── share.py                 # ShareResponse schema\n│   │   ├── marketplace.py           # Marketplace item schemas\n│   │   ├── telemetry.py             # Event schemas\n│   │   ├── models.py                # RooModelsResponse schema\n│   │   └── user.py                  # CloudUserInfo schema\n│   │\n│   ├── routers/                     # FastAPI route modules\n│   │   ├── __init__.py\n│   │   ├── auth.py                  # Clerk-compatible auth facade (/v1/...)\n│   │   ├── extension.py             # /api/extension/* endpoints\n│   │   ├── settings.py              # /api/extension-settings, /api/user-settings\n│   │   ├── events.py                # /api/events, /api/events/backfill\n│   │   ├── marketplace.py           # /api/marketplace/*\n│   │   ├── proxy.py                 # /v1/chat/completions, /v1/models, /v1/images/generations\n│   │   └── browser.py               # /extension/sign-in, /extension/provider-sign-up, /l/*\n│   │\n│   ├── services/                    # Business logic layer\n│   │   ├── __init__.py\n│   │   ├── auth_service.py          # Auth logic: sign-in, session, JWT issuance\n│   │   ├── user_service.py          # User/org CRUD\n│   │   ├── settings_service.py      # Settings fetch/update\n│   │   ├── share_service.py         # Task sharing\n│   │   ├── telemetry_service.py     # Event recording + backfill\n│   │   ├── marketplace_service.py   # Marketplace data loading\n│   │   ├── proxy_service.py         # LLM proxy forwarding\n│   │   └── bridge_service.py        # WebSocket bridge config\n│   │\n│   ├── auth/                        # Auth-specific modules\n│   │   ├── __init__.py\n│   │   ├── authentik.py             # Authentik OAuth client\n│   │   ├── jwt_issuer.py            # Clerk-compatible JWT creation\n│   │   ├── clerk_facade.py          # Clerk API response formatting\n│   │   └── static_token.py          # ROO_CODE_CLOUD_TOKEN validation\n│   │\n│   ├── proxy/                       # LLM proxy modules\n│   │   ├── __init__.py\n│   │   ├── router.py                # Provider routing logic\n│   │   ├── openai_compat.py         # OpenAI-compatible response adapter\n│   │   └── providers/               # Upstream provider clients\n│   │       ├── __init__.py\n│   │       ├── base.py              # Base provider interface\n│   │       ├── openai.py            # OpenAI provider\n│   │       ├── anthropic.py         # Anthropic provider\n│   │       └── custom.py            # Custom/OpenAI-compatible endpoints\n│   │\n│   ├── database.py                  # SQLAlchemy engine, session factory\n│   └── middleware/\n│       ├── __init__.py\n│       ├── rate_limit.py            # Rate limiting middleware\n│       ├── cors.py                  # CORS configuration\n│       └── request_logging.py       # Request/response logging\n│\n└── tests/\n    ├── __init__.py\n    ├── conftest.py                  # Fixtures, test DB\n    ├── test_auth.py\n    ├── test_settings.py\n    ├── test_share.py\n    ├── test_events.py\n    ├── test_marketplace.py\n    ├── test_proxy.py\n    └── test_jwt_issuer.py\n`\n\n---\n\n## 3. Authentication System — Clerk-Compatible Facade\n\nThe most critical and complex part of this architecture is implementing a **Clerk-compatible authentication facade** so the existing Roo Code client works without modification. The client's [`WebAuthService`](packages/cloud/src/WebAuthService.ts) calls specific Clerk API endpoints with exact request/response formats.\n\n### 3.1 Auth Flow Sequence\n\n`mermaid\nsequenceDiagram\n    participant Client as Roo Code Client\n    participant Browser as User Browser\n    participant API as Self-Hosted API\n    participant Authentik as Authentik\n\n    Note over Client: 1. User triggers sign-in\n    Client->>Client: Generate CSRF state, store in globalState\n    Client->>Browser: Open {API_URL}/extension/sign-in?state={csrf}&auth_redirect={vscode://...}\n\n    Browser->>API: GET /extension/sign-in?state={csrf}&auth_redirect={vscode://...}\n    API->>API: Store state + redirect in session\n    API->>Browser: 302 Redirect to Authentik /authorize\n\n    Browser->>Authentik: OAuth Authorize Request\n    Authentik->>Browser: Login UI if needed\n    Browser->>Authentik: User authenticates\n    Authentik->>Browser: 302 Redirect to /auth/clerk/callback?code={authz_code}&state={...}\n\n    Browser->>API: GET /auth/clerk/callback?code={authz_code}\n    API->>Authentik: POST /oauth/token with code + PKCE verifier\n    Authentik->>API: Access token + ID token + refresh token\n    API->>API: Create/update User in DB\n    API->>API: Create Session + ClientToken in DB\n    API->>API: Generate ticket code, store mapping to session\n    API->>Browser: 302 Redirect to auth_redirect URI with code={ticket}&state={csrf}&organizationId={orgId}\n\n    Browser->>Client: VS Code opens URI: vscode://.../auth/clerk/callback?code={ticket}&state={csrf}\n\n    Note over Client: 2. Client exchanges ticket for session\n    Client->>API: POST /v1/client/sign_ins Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded Body: strategy=ticket&ticket={ticket}\n    API->>API: Validate ticket, lookup session\n    API->>Client: 200 {response: {created_session_id: sessionId}} + Authorization header with clientToken\n\n    Note over Client: 3. Client refreshes JWT every ~50s\n    Client->>API: POST /v1/client/sessions/{sessionId}/tokens Body: _is_native=1&organization_id={orgId} Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}\n    API->>API: Generate Clerk-compatible JWT\n    API->>Client: 200 {jwt: encodedJWT}\n\n    Note over Client: 4. Client fetches user info\n    Client->>API: GET /v1/me Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}\n    API->>Client: 200 {response: {id, first_name, last_name, image_url, email_addresses, ...}}\n\n    Client->>API: GET /v1/me/organization_memberships Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}\n    API->>Client: 200 {response: [{id, role, organization: {id, name, slug, image_url, ...}}]}\n`\n\n### 3.2 Clerk-Compatible JWT Payload\n\nThe JWT must match the exact structure the client validates via [`JWTPayload`](packages/types/src/cloud.ts:17). The [`StaticTokenAuthService`](packages/cloud/src/StaticTokenAuthService.ts) decodes the JWT and extracts `r.u`, `r.o`, and `r.t`:\n\n`python\n# JWT claims structure\n{\n    \"iss\": \"rcc\",                    # Issuer — must be \"rcc\"\n    \"sub\": \"user_2xmBhejNeDTwanM8\",  # Subject — user ID for auth tokens\n    \"exp\": 1746200000,               # Expiration (epoch seconds)\n    \"iat\": 1746199500,               # Issued at\n    \"nbf\": 1746199500,               # Not before\n    \"v\": 1,                          # Version — must be 1\n    \"r\": {\n        \"u\": \"user_2xmBhejNeDTwanM8\",  # User ID (always present)\n        \"o\": \"org_2wbhchVXZMQl8OS1\",   # Organization ID (optional, absent when null)\n        \"t\": \"auth\"                     # Token type: \"auth\" for session tokens, \"cj\" for job tokens\n    }\n}\n`\n\n**Key implementation details:**\n- The `iss` field must be `\"rcc\"` — the client may validate this\n- The `r.t` field must be `\"auth\"` for regular session tokens\n- The `r.o` field should be **absent** (not `null`) when the user has no organization context\n- The `sub` field equals the user ID for auth tokens\n- JWTs are signed with an asymmetric key (RS256) or a shared secret (HS256) — configurable\n\n### 3.3 Clerk API Endpoint Implementations\n\n#### `POST /v1/client/sign_ins` — Sign In with Ticket\n\nThe client sends `strategy=ticket&ticket={code}` as form-urlencoded data. The server:\n\n1. Looks up the ticket code in the DB (mapped to a session created during OAuth callback)\n2. Validates the ticket hasn't expired (tickets are single-use, short-lived)\n3. Returns the session ID in the response body\n4. Returns a **client token** in the `Authorization` response header\n\n**Response format** (must match [`clerkSignInResponseSchema`](packages/cloud/src/WebAuthService.ts:39)):\n`json\n{\n    \"response\": {\n        \"created_session_id\": \"sess_abc123\"\n    }\n}\n`\n**Response header**: `Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}` — the client extracts this via [`response.headers.get(\"authorization\")`](packages/cloud/src/WebAuthService.ts:550).\n\n#### `POST /v1/client/sessions/{sessionId}/tokens` — Create Session JWT\n\nThe client sends `_is_native=1` and optionally `organization_id` as form-urlencoded. The server:\n\n1. Validates the `clientToken` from the Authorization header\n2. Validates the session exists and belongs to this client\n3. Generates a Clerk-compatible JWT with 60-second expiry\n4. Returns the JWT\n\n**Response format** (must match [`clerkCreateSessionTokenResponseSchema`](packages/cloud/src/WebAuthService.ts:45)):\n`json\n{\n    \"jwt\": \"eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIs...\"\n}\n`\n\n#### `GET /v1/me` — Get User Profile\n\nThe client sends the `clientToken` in the Authorization header. The server:\n\n1. Validates the client token\n2. Returns user profile data\n\n**Response format** (must match [`clerkMeResponseSchema`](packages/cloud/src/WebAuthService.ts:49)):\n`json\n{\n    \"response\": {\n        \"id\": \"user_abc123\",\n        \"first_name\": \"John\",\n        \"last_name\": \"Doe\",\n        \"image_url\": \"https://...\",\n        \"primary_email_address_id\": \"email_abc\",\n        \"email_addresses\": [\n            {\"id\": \"email_abc\", \"email_address\": \"john@example.com\"}\n        ],\n        \"public_metadata\": {}\n    }\n}\n`\n\n#### `GET /v1/me/organization_memberships` — Get Org Memberships\n\n**Response format** (must match [`clerkOrganizationMembershipsSchema`](packages/cloud/src/WebAuthService.ts:68)):\n`json\n{\n    \"response\": [\n        {\n            \"id\": \"mem_abc123\",\n            \"role\": \"org:admin\",\n            \"permissions\": [\"org:manage:settings\"],\n            \"organization\": {\n                \"id\": \"org_abc123\",\n                \"name\": \"My Org\",\n                \"slug\": \"my-org\",\n                \"image_url\": \"https://...\",\n                \"has_image\": true,\n                \"created_at\": 1700000000,\n                \"updated_at\": 1700000000\n            }\n        }\n    ]\n}\n`\n\n#### `POST /v1/client/sessions/{sessionId}/remove` — Logout\n\nThe client sends `_is_native=1` as form-urlencoded with the clientToken. The server invalidates the session.\n\n### 3.4 Browser Sign-In/Sign-Up Routes\n\nThese routes serve the browser-based authentication flow. The client opens these URLs in the user's browser:\n\n| Route | Purpose |\n|---|---|\n| `GET /extension/sign-in?state={csrf}&auth_redirect={vscode://...}` | Standard sign-in flow |\n| `GET /extension/provider-sign-up?state={csrf}&auth_redirect={vscode://...}` | Provider sign-up flow |\n| `GET /l/{slug}?state={csrf}&auth_redirect={vscode://...}` | Landing page sign-in flow |\n\nAll three routes follow the same pattern:\n1. Store `state` and `auth_redirect` in a server-side session (cookie or Redis)\n2. Redirect to Authentik's `/authorize` endpoint with PKCE code challenge\n3. On Authentik callback, exchange authorization code for tokens\n4. Create user/session/client_token records in DB\n5. Generate a single-use ticket code\n6. Redirect to `auth_redirect` URI with `code={ticket}&state={csrf}&organizationId={orgId}`\n\nThe callback URL that Authentik redirects to must be: `{API_URL}/auth/clerk/callback`\n\nThis matches the client's URI handler at [`/auth/clerk/callback`](src/activate/handleUri.ts:32) which extracts `code`, `state`, `organizationId`, and `provider_model` from the query parameters.\n\n### 3.5 Static Token Support\n\nFor agent/CI use cases, the `ROO_CODE_CLOUD_TOKEN` environment variable provides a pre-issued JWT. The [`StaticTokenAuthService`](packages/cloud/src/StaticTokenAuthService.ts) decodes this JWT directly — it never calls Clerk endpoints. The self-hosted API must:\n\n1. Accept these static tokens as `Bearer` tokens on all API endpoints\n2. Validate the JWT signature and claims\n3. Extract `r.u` (user ID), `r.o` (org ID), and `r.t` (token type) from the JWT\n4. Support token type `\"auth\"` for regular tokens and `\"cj\"` for cloud job tokens\n\n### 3.6 Authentik OAuth Integration\n\n`mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    A[User clicks Sign In] --> B[API redirects to Authentik /authorize]\n    B --> C[Authentik shows login UI]\n    C --> D[Authentik redirects to /auth/clerk/callback with authz code]\n    D --> E[API exchanges code for tokens using PKCE]\n    E --> F[API creates/updates User in DB]\n    F --> G[API creates Session + ClientToken in DB]\n    G --> H[API generates ticket code]\n    H --> I[API redirects to vscode:// URI with ticket code]\n`\n\n**Authentik configuration requirements:**\n- Create an OAuth2 provider with `authorization_code` + `PKCE` flow\n- Configure redirect URI: `{API_URL}/auth/clerk/callback`\n- Map Authentik user attributes to Clerk-compatible user profile fields\n- Configure Authentik to include `email`, `name`, `groups` in ID token claims\n\n---\n\n## 4. Database Schema\n\nAll tables use UUID primary keys with prefix-based string IDs (e.g., `user*`, `sess*`, `org*`) to maintain Clerk API compatibility.\n\n### 4.1 Entity Relationship Diagram\n\n`mermaid\nerDiagram\n    users ||--o{ sessions : has\n    users ||--o{ memberships : belongs_to\n    organizations ||--o{ memberships : has\n    organizations ||--o{ org_settings : has\n    users ||--o{ user_settings : has\n    sessions ||--o{ client_tokens : has\n    users ||--o{ tasks : owns\n    tasks ||--o{ task_messages : contains\n    tasks ||--o{ task_shares : has\n    users ||--o{ telemetry_events : generates\n    organizations ||--o{ provider_configs : has\n`\n\n### 4.2 Table Definitions\n\n#### `users`\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE users (\n id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT ('user*' || gen*random_uuid()::text), -- e.g., \"user_2xmBhejNeDTwanM8\"\n authentik_id TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL, -- Authentik user UUID\n email TEXT NOT NULL,\n first_name TEXT DEFAULT '',\n last_name TEXT DEFAULT '',\n image_url TEXT,\n public_metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n``\n\n#### `organizations`\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE organizations (\n id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT ('org*' || gen*random_uuid()::text),\n name TEXT NOT NULL,\n slug TEXT UNIQUE,\n image_url TEXT,\n has_image BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n``\n\n#### `memberships`\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE memberships (\n id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT ('mem*' || gen*random_uuid()::text),\n user_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n organization_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES organizations(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n role TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'org:member', -- e.g., \"org:admin\", \"org:member\"\n permissions JSONB DEFAULT '[]',\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n UNIQUE(user_id, organization_id)\n);\n``\n\n#### `sessions`\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE sessions (\n id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT ('sess*' || gen*random_uuid()::text),\n user_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ,\n is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE\n);\n``\n\n#### `client*tokens`\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE client_tokens (\n id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT ('ct*' || gen*random_uuid()::text),\n session_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES sessions(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n token_hash TEXT NOT NULL, -- SHA-256 hash of the client token\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ\n);\n``\n\n#### `tickets` (short-lived, single-use)\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE tickets (\n code TEXT PRIMARY KEY, -- The ticket code exchanged at /v1/client/sign_ins\n session_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES sessions(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL, -- Short TTL, e.g., 5 minutes\n used BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE\n);\n``\n\n#### `organization_settings`\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE organization_settings (\n id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT ('os*' || gen*random_uuid()::text),\n organization_id TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL REFERENCES organizations(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n version INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n -- Cloud settings\n record_task_messages BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,\n enable_task_sharing BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,\n allow_public_task_sharing BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,\n task_share_expiration_days INTEGER DEFAULT 30,\n allow_members_view_all_tasks BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,\n workspace_task_visibility TEXT DEFAULT 'all',\n llm_enhanced_features_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,\n -- Default settings (JSONB for flexibility)\n default_settings JSONB DEFAULT '{}',\n -- Allow list\n allow_list JSONB DEFAULT '{\"allowAll\": true, \"providers\": {}}',\n -- Features\n features JSONB DEFAULT '{}',\n -- MCPs and marketplace\n hidden_mcps TEXT[] DEFAULT '{}',\n hide_marketplace_mcps BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,\n mcps JSONB DEFAULT '[]',\n -- Provider profiles\n provider_profiles JSONB DEFAULT '{}',\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n``\n\n#### `user_settings`\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE user_settings (\n id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT ('us*' || gen*random_uuid()::text),\n user_id TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n features JSONB DEFAULT '{}',\n settings JSONB DEFAULT '{}', -- {taskSyncEnabled, llmEnhancedFeaturesEnabled}\n version INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n``\n\n#### `tasks`\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE tasks (\n id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n user_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n organization_id TEXT REFERENCES organizations(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n``\n\n#### `task_messages`\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE task_messages (\n id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT ('msg*' || gen*random_uuid()::text),\n task_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES tasks(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n message_data JSONB NOT NULL, -- Full ClineMessage JSON\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n``\n\n#### `task_shares`\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE task_shares (\n id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT ('sh*' || gen*random_uuid()::text),\n task_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES tasks(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n visibility TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'organization', -- 'organization' or 'public'\n share_url TEXT,\n manage_url TEXT,\n expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ,\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n``\n\n#### `telemetry_events`\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE telemetry_events (\n id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT ('evt*' || gen*random_uuid()::text),\n user_id TEXT REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,\n organization_id TEXT REFERENCES organizations(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,\n event_type TEXT NOT NULL,\n properties JSONB DEFAULT '{}',\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n``\n\n#### `provider_configs` (LLM proxy configuration)\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE provider_configs (\n id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT ('pc*' || gen*random_uuid()::text),\n organization_id TEXT UNIQUE REFERENCES organizations(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n providers JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]', -- List of provider configs\n model_overrides JSONB DEFAULT '{}', -- Per-model overrides\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()\n);\n``\n\n#### `authentik_state_store` (OAuth state + PKCE verifiers)\n``sql\nCREATE TABLE authentik_state_store (\n state TEXT PRIMARY KEY, -- CSRF state parameter\n auth_redirect TEXT NOT NULL, -- VS Code URI to redirect back to\n code_verifier TEXT NOT NULL, -- PKCE code verifier\n created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),\n expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL -- Short TTL, e.g., 10 minutes\n);\n``\n\n---\n\n## 5. API Layer — FastAPI Routers\n\n### 5.1 Router Overview\n\n| Router | Prefix | Endpoints |\n|---|---|---|\n| `auth.py` | `/v1` | Clerk-compatible auth endpoints |\n| `extension.py` | `/api/extension` | Share, bridge config, credit balance |\n| `settings.py` | `/api` | Extension settings, user settings |\n| `events.py` | `/api` | Telemetry events, backfill |\n| `marketplace.py` | `/api/marketplace` | Mode/MCP marketplace |\n| `proxy.py` | `/v1` | LLM proxy endpoints |\n| `browser.py` | `/extension`, `/l`, `/auth/clerk/callback` | Browser auth flows |\n\n### 5.2 Auth Router — Clerk-Compatible Endpoints\n\n``python\n# routers/auth.py\n\nrouter = APIRouter(prefix=\"/v1\")\n\n@router.post(\"/client/sign_ins\")\nasync def sign_in(request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Clerk-compatible sign-in endpoint.\n Accepts form-urlencoded: strategy=ticket&ticket={code}\n Returns: { response: { created_session_id: \"sess*...\" } }\n Header: Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}\n \"\"\"\n\n@router.post(\"/client/sessions/{session*id}/tokens\")\nasync def create_session_token(session_id: str, request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Clerk-compatible session token creation.\n Accepts form-urlencoded: \_is_native=1&organization_id={orgId}\n Header: Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}\n Returns: { jwt: \"...\" }\n \"\"\"\n\n@router.get(\"/me\")\nasync def get_me(request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Clerk-compatible user profile endpoint.\n Header: Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}\n Returns: { response: { id, first_name, last_name, image_url, ... } }\n \"\"\"\n\n@router.get(\"/me/organization_memberships\")\nasync def get_organization_memberships(request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Clerk-compatible org memberships endpoint.\n Header: Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}\n Returns: { response: [{ id, role, organization: { id, name, slug, ... } }] }\n \"\"\"\n\n@router.post(\"/client/sessions/{session_id}/remove\")\nasync def remove_session(session_id: str, request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Clerk-compatible logout endpoint.\n Accepts form-urlencoded: \_is_native=1\n Header: Authorization: Bearer {clientToken}\n \"\"\"\n`\n\n### 5.3 Extension Router\n\n`python\n# routers/extension.py\n\nrouter = APIRouter(prefix=\"/api/extension\")\n\n@router.post(\"/share\")\nasync def share_task(request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Share a task.\n Body: { taskId, visibility }\n Returns: { success, shareUrl, error, isNewShare, manageUrl }\n \"\"\"\n\n@router.get(\"/bridge/config\")\nasync def bridge_config(request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Get bridge/websocket config.\n Returns: { userId, socketBridgeUrl, token }\n \"\"\"\n\n@router.get(\"/credit-balance\")\nasync def credit_balance(request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Get credit balance.\n Returns: { balance: number }\n \"\"\"\n`\n\n### 5.4 Settings Router\n\n`python\n# routers/settings.py\n\nrouter = APIRouter(prefix=\"/api\")\n\n@router.get(\"/extension-settings\")\nasync def get_extension_settings(request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Fetch org + user settings.\n Returns: { organization: OrganizationSettings, user: UserSettingsData }\n \"\"\"\n\n@router.patch(\"/user-settings\")\nasync def update_user_settings(request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Update user settings.\n Body: { settings, version }\n Returns: UserSettingsData\n Supports optimistic locking via version field.\n \"\"\"\n`\n\n### 5.5 Events Router\n\n`python\n# routers/events.py\n\nrouter = APIRouter(prefix=\"/api\")\n\n@router.post(\"/events\")\nasync def record_event(request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Record telemetry event.\n Body: { type, properties }\n \"\"\"\n\n@router.post(\"/events/backfill\")\nasync def backfill_events(request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Backfill task messages (FormData).\n Body: taskId + properties JSON + file (task.json)\n \"\"\"\n`\n\n### 5.6 Marketplace Router\n\n`python\n# routers/marketplace.py\n\nrouter = APIRouter(prefix=\"/api/marketplace\")\n\n@router.get(\"/modes\")\nasync def get_modes() -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Fetch mode marketplace items.\n Unauthenticated — returns YAML/JSON mode definitions.\n \"\"\"\n\n@router.get(\"/mcps\")\nasync def get_mcps() -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Fetch MCP marketplace items.\n Unauthenticated — returns YAML/JSON MCP definitions.\n \"\"\"\n`\n\n### 5.7 Proxy Router — LLM Proxy\n\n`python\n# routers/proxy.py\n\nrouter = APIRouter(prefix=\"/v1\")\n\n@router.get(\"/models\")\nasync def list_models(request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n List available models.\n Returns RooModelsResponse: { object: \"list\", data: [...] }\n Optional auth: Bearer sessionToken\n \"\"\"\n\n@router.post(\"/chat/completions\")\nasync def chat_completions(request: Request) -> StreamingResponse:\n \"\"\"\n OpenAI-compatible streaming chat completions.\n Auth: Bearer sessionToken\n Forwards to upstream LLM provider.\n \"\"\"\n\n@router.post(\"/images/generations\")\nasync def image_generations(request: Request) -> Response:\n \"\"\"\n Image generation endpoint.\n Auth: Bearer sessionToken\n \"\"\"\n`\n\n### 5.8 Browser Router — Auth Flow Pages\n\n`python\n# routers/browser.py\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n@router.get(\"/extension/sign-in\")\nasync def sign_in_page(state: str, auth_redirect: str):\n \"\"\"Redirect to Authentik OAuth authorize URL.\"\"\"\n\n@router.get(\"/extension/provider-sign-up\")\nasync def provider_sign_up_page(state: str, auth_redirect: str):\n \"\"\"Redirect to Authentik OAuth authorize URL (signup flow).\"\"\"\n\n@router.get(\"/l/{slug}\")\nasync def landing_page(slug: str, state: str, auth_redirect: str):\n \"\"\"Redirect to Authentik OAuth authorize URL (landing page flow).\"\"\"\n\n@router.get(\"/auth/clerk/callback\")\nasync def auth_callback(code: str, state: str):\n \"\"\"\n Authentik OAuth callback.\n Exchange code for tokens, create user/session, generate ticket,\n redirect to auth_redirect URI.\n \"\"\"\n``\n\n---\n\n## 6. LLM Proxy Architecture\n\nThe LLM proxy forwards OpenAI-compatible requests to upstream providers and returns OpenAI-compatible responses. The client's [`RooHandler`](src/api/providers/roo.ts) constructs an OpenAI client pointing at `{ROO_CODE_PROVIDER_URL}/v1`.\n\n### 6.1 Proxy Flow\n\n``mermaid\nflowchart TD\n A[Roo Code Client] -->|POST /v1/chat/completions Bearer token| B[Self-Hosted API Proxy]\n B --> C[Validate JWT / extract user+org]\n C --> D[Lookup provider config for org]\n D --> E{Route to provider}\n E -->|OpenAI| F[OpenAI API]\n E -->|Anthropic| G[Anthropic API]\n E -->|Custom| H[Custom OpenAI-compatible endpoint]\n F --> I[Transform response to OpenAI format]\n G --> I\n H --> I\n I -->|SSE stream| A\n``\n\n### 6.2 Model Configuration\n\nModels are served from the `/v1/models` endpoint and must conform to the [`RooModelsResponseSchema`](packages/types/src/providers/roo.ts:54):\n\n``json\n{\n \"object\": \"list\",\n \"data\": [\n {\n \"id\": \"anthropic/claude-sonnet-4-20250514\",\n \"object\": \"model\",\n \"created\": 1700000000,\n \"owned_by\": \"anthropic\",\n \"name\": \"Claude Sonnet 4\",\n \"description\": \"High-performance model...\",\n \"context_window\": 200000,\n \"max_tokens\": 8192,\n \"type\": \"language\",\n \"tags\": [\"vision\", \"reasoning\"],\n \"pricing\": {\n \"input\": \"0.000003\",\n \"output\": \"0.000015\",\n \"input_cache_read\": \"0.0000003\",\n \"input_cache_write\": \"0.000003\"\n },\n \"deprecated\": false,\n \"default_temperature\": 0.0,\n \"settings\": {},\n \"versionedSettings\": {}\n }\n ]\n}\n``\n\n**Key observations from the client code:**\n- Pricing values are **strings** (not numbers) — the client parses them with [`parseApiPrice`](src/api/providers/fetchers/roo.ts)\n- The `tags` field drives feature detection: `\"vision\"`, `\"reasoning\"`, `\"reasoning-required\"`, `\"stealth\"`, `\"free\"`\n- The `settings` and `versionedSettings` fields allow per-model configuration overrides\n- The `type` field must be `\"language\"`\n\n### 6.3 Provider Routing\n\nThe proxy routes requests based on the model ID prefix:\n\n| Model ID Prefix | Upstream Provider | API Format |\n|---|---|---|\n| `openai/` | OpenAI API | Native OpenAI |\n| `anthropic/` | Anthropic API | Convert to/from OpenAI format |\n| `google/` | Google AI API | Convert to/from OpenAI format |\n| `xai/` | xAI/Grok API | OpenAI-compatible |\n| `custom/` | User-configured endpoint | OpenAI-compatible passthrough |\n\nThe routing configuration is stored per-organization in the `provider_configs` table and can be overridden via environment variables for single-user deployments.\n\n### 6.4 Streaming\n\nThe proxy must support **Server-Sent Events (SSE)** streaming, matching the OpenAI streaming format. The client uses `stream: true` and `stream_options: { include_usage: true }`. The proxy:\n\n1. Receives the streaming request from the client\n2. Forwards it to the upstream provider (converting format if needed)\n3. Streams the response back in OpenAI SSE format\n4. Handles `reasoning_details` in delta chunks (used by newer models)\n\n---\n\n## 7. Configuration\n\n### 7.1 Environment Variables\n\n``bash\n# === Core ===\nDATABASE_URL=postgresql://roo:password@localhost:5432/roo_cloud\nSECRET_KEY=your-secret-key-for-jwt-signing\nJWT_ALGORITHM=RS256 # or HS256\nJWT_PRIVATE_KEY=/path/to/private.pem # For RS256\nJWT_PUBLIC_KEY=/path/to/public.pem # For RS256\nJWT_SECRET=your-hs256-secret # For HS256\n\n# === Authentik OAuth ===\nAUTHENTIK_BASE_URL=https://auth.example.com\nAUTHENTIK_CLIENT_ID=your-client-id\nAUTHENTIK_CLIENT_SECRET=your-client-secret # If not using PKCE\nAUTHENTIK_REDIRECT_URI=https://roo.example.com/auth/clerk/callback\n\n# === API ===\nAPI_BASE_URL=https://roo.example.com # Public URL of this API\nCORS_ORIGINS=https://your-vscode-extension-origin # Or * for development\n\n# === LLM Proxy ===\nDEFAULT_LLM_PROVIDER=openai # Default upstream provider\nOPENAI_API_KEY=sk-...\nANTHROPIC_API_KEY=sk-ant-...\nGOOGLE_API_KEY=...\nXAI_API_KEY=...\n\n# === Marketplace ===\nMARKETPLACE_SOURCE=database # \"database\" or \"yaml\"\nMARKETPLACE_YAML_DIR=/path/to/config/marketplace # If MARKETPLACE_SOURCE=yaml\n\n# === Optional ===\nCREDIT_SYSTEM_ENABLED=false # Enable credit balance tracking\nBRIDGE_ENABLED=false # Enable WebSocket bridge\nTELEMETRY_ENABLED=true # Accept telemetry events\nRATE_LIMIT_ENABLED=true\nRATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS_PER_MINUTE=60\n``\n\n### 7.2 Settings Management\n\nUse Pydantic `BaseSettings` for type-safe configuration:\n\n``python\nclass Settings(BaseSettings):\n database_url: PostgresDsn\n secret_key: str\n jwt_algorithm: str = \"HS256\"\n jwt_private_key: Optional[str] = None\n jwt_public_key: Optional[str] = None\n jwt_secret: Optional[str] = None\n\n authentik_base_url: HttpUrl\n authentik_client_id: str\n authentik_client_secret: Optional[str] = None\n authentik_redirect_uri: HttpUrl\n\n api_base_url: HttpUrl\n cors_origins: List[str] = [\"*\"]\n\n default_llm_provider: str = \"openai\"\n openai_api_key: Optional[str] = None\n anthropic_api_key: Optional[str] = None\n # ... etc\n\n class Config:\n env_file = \".env\"\n env_file_encoding = \"utf-8\"\n`\n\n---\n\n## 8. Docker Deployment\n\n### 8.1 Dockerfile\n\n`dockerfile\nFROM python:3.12-slim\n\nWORKDIR /app\n\n# Install system dependencies\nRUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \\\n build-essential \\\n && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*\n\n# Install Python dependencies\nCOPY pyproject.toml poetry.lock ./\nRUN pip install --no-cache-dir poetry && \\\n poetry config virtualenvs.create false && \\\n poetry install --no-dev --no-interaction --no-ansi\n\n# Copy application\nCOPY . .\n\n# Run Alembic migrations on startup, then start the app\nCMD [\"sh\", \"-c\", \"alembic upgrade head && uvicorn src.main:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000\"]\n`\n\n### 8.2 docker-compose.yml\n\n`yaml\nversion: \"3.8\"\n\nservices:\n api:\n build: .\n ports:\n - \"8000:8000\"\n environment:\n DATABASE_URL: postgresql://roo:password@postgres:5432/roo_cloud\n SECRET_KEY: ${SECRET_KEY}\n JWT_ALGORITHM: ${JWT_ALGORITHM:-HS256}\n JWT_SECRET: ${JWT_SECRET:-}\n AUTHENTIK_BASE_URL: ${AUTHENTIK_BASE_URL}\n AUTHENTIK_CLIENT_ID: ${AUTHENTIK_CLIENT_ID}\n AUTHENTIK_CLIENT_SECRET: ${AUTHENTIK_CLIENT_SECRET}\n AUTHENTIK_REDIRECT_URI: ${AUTHENTIK_REDIRECT_URI}\n API_BASE_URL: ${API_BASE_URL}\n CORS_ORIGINS: ${CORS_ORIGINS:-*}\n OPENAI_API_KEY: ${OPENAI_API_KEY:-}\n ANTHROPIC_API_KEY: ${ANTHROPIC_API_KEY:-}\n depends_on:\n postgres:\n condition: service_healthy\n restart: unless-stopped\n\n postgres:\n image: postgres:16-alpine\n ports:\n - \"5432:5432\"\n environment:\n POSTGRES_USER: roo\n POSTGRES_PASSWORD: password\n POSTGRES_DB: roo_cloud\n volumes:\n - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data\n healthcheck:\n test: [\"CMD-SHELL\", \"pg_isready -U roo\"]\n interval: 5s\n timeout: 5s\n retries: 5\n\n # Authentik - separate docker-compose or external\n # Users should deploy Authentik separately and configure\n # AUTHENTIK_BASE_URL, AUTHENTIK_CLIENT_ID, etc.\n\nvolumes:\n postgres_data:\n``\n\n### 8.3 Authentik Integration Notes\n\nAuthentik should be deployed separately (it has its own docker-compose). The self-hosted API only needs:\n\n1. **Authentik OAuth2 Provider** configured with:\n   - Client ID and secret\n   - Redirect URI: `{API_BASE_URL}/auth/clerk/callback`\n   - Scopes: `openid`, `profile`, `email`\n2. **Authentik User Attributes** mapped to Clerk-compatible fields:\n   - `email` → `email_addresses[0].email_address`\n   - `name` → `first_name` + `last_name`\n   - `picture` → `image_url`\n   - `groups` → organization memberships\n\n---\n\n## 9. Security\n\n### 9.1 CORS\n\n``python\napp.add_middleware(\n CORSMiddleware,\n allow_origins=settings.cors_origins,\n allow_credentials=True,\n allow_methods=[\"*\"],\n allow_headers=[\"*\"],\n)\n``\n\n### 9.2 Rate Limiting\n\nUse `slowapi` or a custom middleware:\n\n``python\nfrom slowapi import Limiter\nlimiter = Limiter(key_func=get_remote_address)\napp.state.limiter = limiter\n``\n\nRate limits per endpoint:\n- Auth endpoints: 10 requests/minute\n- API endpoints: 60 requests/minute\n- Proxy endpoints: 100 requests/minute (per user)\n- Marketplace: 30 requests/minute\n\n### 9.3 Input Validation\n\nAll request bodies validated with Pydantic schemas matching the client's Zod schemas:\n\n- [`shareResponseSchema`](packages/types/src/cloud.ts:223) → `ShareResponseSchema`\n- [`organizationSettingsSchema`](packages/types/src/cloud.ts:153) → `OrganizationSettingsSchema`\n- [`userSettingsDataSchema`](packages/types/src/cloud.ts:182) → `UserSettingsDataSchema`\n- [`RooModelsResponseSchema`](packages/types/src/providers/roo.ts:54) → `ModelsResponseSchema`\n\n### 9.4 JWT Security\n\n- JWTs signed with RS256 (asymmetric) by default; HS256 supported for simpler deployments\n- Client tokens are SHA-256 hashed before storage\n- Tickets are single-use and expire within 5 minutes\n- Session JWTs expire every 60 seconds (client refreshes every ~50 seconds)\n- Static tokens (`ROO_CODE_CLOUD_TOKEN`) validated against the same JWT signature\n\n### 9.5 SQL Injection Prevention\n\nAll database queries use SQLAlchemy ORM with parameterized queries. No raw SQL.\n\n---\n\n## 10. Marketplace\n\nThe marketplace endpoints serve mode and MCP definitions. Two strategies are supported:\n\n### 10.1 YAML File Mode (Default for Self-Hosted)\n\nMarketplace items are defined in YAML files under `config/marketplace/`:\n\n``yaml\n# config/marketplace/modes.yaml\n- id: code-mode\n name: Code\n description: \"Optimized for code writing and editing\"\n type: mode\n content: |\n # Code Mode Configuration\n ...\n- id: architect-mode\n name: Architect\n description: \"Optimized for planning and architecture\"\n type: mode\n content: |\n # Architect Mode Configuration\n ...\n`\n\n`yaml\n# config/marketplace/mcps.yaml\n- id: filesystem-mcp\n name: Filesystem\n description: \"File system access MCP server\"\n type: mcp\n url: \"https://github.com/...\"\n```\n\n### 10.2 Database Mode\n\nFor multi-tenant deployments, marketplace items are stored in a `marketplace_entries` table and managed via admin API endpoints.\n\n### 10.3 Organization Filtering\n\nWhen authenticated, the API applies organization-level filtering:\n- `hiddenMcps` from org settings are removed from MCP marketplace results\n- `hideMarketplaceMcps` flag can suppress all MCP marketplace items\n- Organization-specific MCPs from org settings are prepended to results\n\nThis matches the client behavior in [`MarketplaceManager`](src/services/marketplace/MarketplaceManager.ts).\n\n---\n\n## 11. Implementation Phases\n\n### Phase 1: Core Auth + API Skeleton\n- [ ] Set up FastAPI project structure with SQLAlchemy + Alembic\n- [ ] Implement database schema (users, sessions, client_tokens, tickets, organizations, memberships)\n- [ ] Implement Authentik OAuth flow (browser sign-in, callback, ticket generation)\n- [ ] Implement Clerk-compatible auth facade (all 5 endpoints)\n- [ ] Implement JWT issuance with exact payload structure\n- [ ] Implement static token validation\n- [ ] Docker + docker-compose setup\n- [ ] Integration test: client can authenticate end-to-end\n\n### Phase 2: Settings + Extension API\n- [ ] Implement organization settings CRUD\n- [ ] Implement user settings CRUD with optimistic locking\n- [ ] Implement `/api/extension-settings` endpoint\n- [ ] Implement `/api/user-settings` PATCH endpoint\n- [ ] Implement `/api/extension/share` endpoint\n- [ ] Implement `/api/extension/bridge/config` endpoint\n- [ ] Implement `/api/extension/credit-balance` endpoint\n\n### Phase 3: Telemetry + Marketplace\n- [ ] Implement `/api/events` POST endpoint\n- [ ] Implement `/api/events/backfill` POST endpoint\n- [ ] Implement marketplace YAML loading\n- [ ] Implement `/api/marketplace/modes` endpoint\n- [ ] Implement `/api/marketplace/mcps` endpoint\n- [ ] Implement org-level marketplace filtering\n\n### Phase 4: LLM Proxy\n- [ ] Implement `/v1/models` endpoint with configurable model catalog\n- [ ] Implement `/v1/chat/completions` streaming proxy\n- [ ] Implement provider routing (OpenAI, Anthropic, custom)\n- [ ] Implement `/v1/images/generations` proxy\n- [ ] Implement request/response format conversion for non-OpenAI providers\n- [ ] Implement usage tracking and rate limiting per org\n\n### Phase 5: Polish + Production Readiness\n- [ ] Comprehensive test coverage\n- [ ] Admin API for user/org/model management\n- [ ] Database migrations for all schema changes\n- [ ] Monitoring and health checks\n- [ ] Documentation and deployment guide\n- [ ] Security audit\n\n---\n\n## 12. Key Design Decisions\n\n### 12.1 Why Clerk-Compatible Facade Instead of Modifying the Client?\n\nThe existing [`WebAuthService`](packages/cloud/src/WebAuthService.ts) in the Roo Code client makes specific HTTP calls to Clerk-formatted endpoints with exact request/response schemas. Modifying the client would require:\n1. Forking and maintaining the extension\n2. Breaking compatibility with the official Roo Code Cloud\n3. Requiring all users to install a custom build\n\nBy implementing a Clerk-compatible facade, users can point `CLERK_BASE_URL` to the self-hosted API and use the **unmodified** official extension.\n\n### 12.2 Why Authentik Instead of Building Custom Auth?\n\nAuthentik provides:\n- Production-grade OAuth2/OIDC provider\n- User management UI\n- SSO, MFA, and directory sync\n- Docker deployment\n- No need to build login UI, password reset, email verification, etc.\n\nThe self-hosted API only needs to bridge Authentik's OAuth flow to Clerk's API format.\n\n### 12.3 Why PostgreSQL + SQLAlchemy?\n\n- PostgreSQL provides robust relational storage with JSONB for flexible schema fields\n- SQLAlchemy ORM provides type-safe queries and migration support via Alembic\n- Matches the production Roo Code Cloud stack for easier compatibility testing\n\n### 12.4 Why Separate Browser Auth Routes from Clerk API Routes?\n\nThe browser routes (`/extension/sign-in`, `/auth/clerk/callback`) handle the **OAuth redirect flow** — they are visited by the user's browser. The Clerk API routes (`/v1/client/sign_ins`, etc.) are called by the **VS Code extension** programmatically. Keeping them separate ensures clean separation of concerns and makes the auth flow debuggable."
}
